var isNonSubcribed = true;
var UserStatus = "anonymous";

function createCookie(name,value,days) { if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}
function eraseCookie(name) {
createCookie(name,"",-1);
}
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
return null;
}
function deleteCookie(name) {
createCookiewithdomain(name,null,-1);
}
function createCookiewithdomain(name,value,days) {
if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; domain="+document.location.host.match(/\.[.\w]*/)+";path=/";
}
function getStorage(name){	if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {	if (localStorage.getItem(name)){	cookieObj = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(name));
if (cookieObj !== undefined && (cookieObj.e == null || cookieObj.e > new Date())){return cookieObj.v === undefined ? null : cookieObj.v ; }	else{localStorage.removeItem(name);}	}
return null;	} else {return readCookie(name);}	}
function setStorage(name,value,days){
if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {
var date = new Date();	localStorage.setItem(name,JSON.stringify({"v":value, "e":date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000))}))
} else {createCookie(name,value,days);}	}
function eraseStorage(name){ if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {localStorage.removeItem(name);}
else{eraseCookie(name)}
}
function getUrlParameter( name, url ) {
if (!url) url = location.href;
name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
var regex = new RegExp(regexS,"i");
var results = regex.exec( url );
return results == null ? null : results[1];
}
function getHostName(){
return window.location.hostname;
} function loadAsyncURL(url){ var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
s.type = "text/javascript";
s.async = true; s.src = url; el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
}
function loadSyncURL(url){ var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
s.type = "text/javascript";
s.src = url; el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
}
function loadPromiseScript(src) {
return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
let script = document.createElement('script');
script.src = src;
script.async = true;
script.onload = function(){
resolve(script);
}
document.head.append(script);
});
}
function crossfetchGet(url,fn){
// Default options are marked with *
return fetch(url, {
method: 'GET', // *GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, etc.
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include', // include, *same-origin, omit
}).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.reject();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.reject();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}	function crossfetchPost(url, data, fn) {
return fetch(url, {
method: 'POST',
body: JSON.stringify(data),
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include', // include, *same-origin, omit
}).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}
function fetchtimeout(ms,url,options,fn) {
const FETCH_TIMEOUT = ms;
let didTimeOut = false;
return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
const timeout = setTimeout(function() {
didTimeOut = true;
reject(new Error('Request timed out -> ' +ms +" ms"));
}, FETCH_TIMEOUT);
fetch(url,options).then(function(response) {
// Clear the timeout as cleanup
clearTimeout(timeout);
if(!didTimeOut) {
resolve(response);
}
})
.catch(function(err) {
// Rejection already happened with setTimeout
if(didTimeOut) return;
// Reject with error
reject(err);
//	console.error(err.message +"= "+url);
})
}).then(function(response) {
// Request success and no timeout
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else
{
console.error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText); }
})
.then(function(response) {
fn(response);
})
.catch(function(err) {
// Error: response error, request timeout or runtime error
console.error(err.message +"= "+url);
return Promise.resolve();
//return Promise.reject();
})
}
function fetchApi(url,options,fn) {
return fetch(url,options).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}

         <script>
          require(['jquery','jqueryui'], function ($){
$(document).ready(function() {
$("input.form-control.tracktag").autocomplete({
minLength: 3,
position: { my : "right top", at: "right bottom" },
delay: 50,
source: function(request, response) {
var timeDelay = 500;
setTimeout(loadXML, timeDelay);
function loadXML() {
$.ajax({
url: "https://www.thehindubusinessline.com/s/t/?q=" + request.term,
success: function(data) {
var r = data;
if (r.status == "SUCCESS") {
response($.map(r.data, function(dataItem) {
return {
label: __highlight(dataItem.title, request.term),
value: dataItem.title,
url: dataItem.url + "/overview/",
path: dataItem.path
};
}));
} else {
var result = [{
label: 'No matches found',
url:"",
value: response.term
}];
response(result);
}
}
});
}
},
select: function(event, ui) {
event.preventDefault();
if (ui.item.url != "") {
window.open(ui.item.url);
}
}
}).each(function() {
$(this).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
return $("<li></li>")
.data("item.autocomplete", item)
.append($("<a'></a>").html(item.label))
.appendTo(ul);
};
});
function __highlight(s, t) {
var matcher = new RegExp("(" + $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(t) + ")", "ig");
return s.replace(matcher, "<span style='color:#144D94;font-weight: bold;'>$1</span>");
}
});
});
         </script>

        require(['jquery','jqueryui'], function ($){
$(document).ready(function() {
$("input.form-control.tracktag").autocomplete({
minLength: 3,
position: { my : "right top", at: "right bottom" },
delay: 50,
source: function(request, response) {
var timeDelay = 500;
setTimeout(loadXML, timeDelay);
function loadXML() {
$.ajax({
url: "https://www.thehindubusinessline.com/s/t/?q=" + request.term,
success: function(data) {
var r = data;
if (r.status == "SUCCESS") {
response($.map(r.data, function(dataItem) {
return {
label: __highlight(dataItem.title, request.term),
value: dataItem.title,
url: dataItem.url + "/overview/",
path: dataItem.path
};
}));
} else {
var result = [{
label: 'No matches found',
url:"",
value: response.term
}];
response(result);
}
}
});
}
},
select: function(event, ui) {
event.preventDefault();
if (ui.item.url != "") {
window.open(ui.item.url);
}
}
}).each(function() {
$(this).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
return $("<li></li>")
.data("item.autocomplete", item)
.append($("<a'></a>").html(item.label))
.appendTo(ul);
};
});
function __highlight(s, t) {
var matcher = new RegExp("(" + $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(t) + ")", "ig");
return s.replace(matcher, "<span style='color:#144D94;font-weight: bold;'>$1</span>");
}
});
});
       </script>

         <script>
          require(['swiper'],function(swiper){
$(function(){
function setCurrentSlide(ele,index){
$(".stockshead .swiper-slide").removeClass("selected");
ele.addClass("selected");
}
var stockshead = new Swiper('.stockshead', {
slidesPerView: 2,
spaceBetween: 15,	loop: false , normalizeSlideIndex:false
});
$(".stock-button-next").on('click',function(){
stocksbody.slideNext();	});
$(".stock-button-prev").on('click',function(){
stocksbody.slidePrev();	});
$(".stockshead .swiper-slide").on('click',function(){
var n = $(".stockshead .swiper-slide").index($(this));
stocksbody.slideTo(n , 500, false);
stockshead.slideTo(n , 500, false);
});
var stocksbody = new Swiper ('.stocksbody', {
direction: 'horizontal',	loop: false,	autoHeight: true,
allowSlideNext:false,
allowSlidePrev:false,
onSlideChangeStart: function(swiper){
var n=swiper.activeIndex + 1; stockshead.slideTo(n - 1, 500, false);
$(".stockshead .swiper-slide").removeClass("selected");
$(".stockshead .swiper-slide:nth-child(" + n + ")").addClass("selected");
}
});
}); });
         </script>

    <script data-cfasync="false">
     async function eagerLoading(){
var sizes = imageSizes;
var imgSelector = "img.adaptive.lazy";
var position = 0;
for ( var type in WFClientTypeDef) {
if (window.matchMedia(WFClientTypeDef[type]).matches) {
switch (type) {
case "xlarge":
position = 0;
break;
case "large":
position = 1;
break;
case "medium":
position = 2;
break;
case "small":
position = 3;
break;
}
break;
}
}
var elements = document.querySelectorAll(imgSelector);
Array.prototype.slice.call(elements).slice(0,2).forEach(function(el, i){	var template = el.getAttribute('data-src-template');
if (template == null) {
return;
}
var prevWidth = el.getAttribute('data-selected-width');
if (prevWidth !== null) {
return;
}
var variant = el.getAttribute('data-variant');
var customVariant = variant+"~"+el.getAttribute('data-device-variant');
if("" != el.getAttribute('data-device-variant'))
variant = customVariant.split("~")[position];	var elementWidth = el.offsetWidth;
var selected = Math.max.apply(null, sizes);
for (var i = 0; i < sizes.length; i++) {
if (elementWidth <= sizes[i]) {
selected = sizes[i];
break;
}
} if (prevWidth && prevWidth >= selected) {
return;
}	el.setAttribute('data-selected-width',selected);
var binaryRegEx = new RegExp("/binary/", "ig");
var thumbnailRegEx = new RegExp("/thumbnail/", "ig");
var adaptedSrc = template.replace(binaryRegEx, "/alternates/").replace(thumbnailRegEx, "/" + variant + "_" + selected + "/");
el.setAttribute('src',appURL() + "static/img/placeholder/" + variant + ".gif"); el.setAttribute('src', adaptedSrc);	}
);
}
if(typeof(eagerLoading) == 'function'){eagerLoading();}
    </script>

         <script>
          var emailAddressFilter = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/;
function validate_email(fieldId) {
var email = $(fieldId).val();
email= email.trim();
if (email == "" || email == "undefined") {
return false;
}else if (!emailAddressFilter.test(email)) {
return false;
}
return true;
}
$(document).ready(function(){
$(".Subscribe").each(function() {
var id = "div."+$(this).attr("class");
$(id + " button#nwemail_button").on("click", function(event){
$(id + " button").attr("disabled","disabled");
$(id + " input").click(function(){$(id + " button").removeAttr("disabled");});
var email = $(id +" input").val();
email= email.trim();
$(id + " #nwemail_error").css("display", "none");
$(id + " #nwemail_success").css("display", "none");
$(id + " input").removeClass("error");
if (validate_email(id + " input") ){
$(id + " #newsletter_load").show();
var data = {	"email" : email, "category" : "newsletter"};
$.ajax({
type : "POST",
contentType : "application/json",
url : publist("url") + "s/mailsubscription/subscribe/",
data : JSON.stringify(data),
dataType : 'json',
timeout : 10000,
success : function(response) {
// console.log("SUCCESS: ", response);
$(id + " #nwemail_success").html("<p>"+response.data+"</p>");
$(id + " #nwemail_success").css("display", "block");
$(id + " #newsletter_load").hide();
},
error : function(e) {
// console.log("ERROR: ", e);
},
done : function(e) {
// console.log("DONE");
}
});
} else {
$(id + " #newsletter_load").fadeOut( "slow");$(id + " #nwemail_error").css("display", "block");
$(id + " input").addClass("error");
}
});
});
});
         </script>

if (aUrl && aUrl.match(/article(\d+).ece$/)) {

return true;
} else {
return false;
}

         <script>
          function overlayControll (evt) {
if(evt.origin === 'https://creatives.thehindu.com'){
document.querySelector("#ppoverlay").style.display = "none";
}
}
if (window.addEventListener) {
window.addEventListener("message", overlayControll, false);
}
else {
window.attachEvent("onmessage", overlayControll);
}
         </script>

              </a>
             </article>

                 <input class="form-control tracktag" id="srch-term01" name="" placeholder="TRACK YOUR STOCKS" type="text"/>
                </div>
               </form>
               <script>
                require(['jquery','jqueryui'], function ($){
$(document).ready(function() {
$("input.form-control.tracktag").autocomplete({
minLength: 3,
position: { my : "right top", at: "right bottom" },
delay: 50,
source: function(request, response) {
var timeDelay = 500;
setTimeout(loadXML, timeDelay);
function loadXML() {
$.ajax({
url: "https://www.thehindubusinessline.com/s/t/?q=" + request.term,
success: function(data) {
var r = data;
if (r.status == "SUCCESS") {
response($.map(r.data, function(dataItem) {
return {
label: __highlight(dataItem.title, request.term),
value: dataItem.title,
url: dataItem.url + "/overview/",
path: dataItem.path
};
}));
} else {
var result = [{
label: 'No matches found',
url:"",
value: response.term
}];
response(result);
}
}
});
}
},
select: function(event, ui) {
event.preventDefault();
if (ui.item.url != "") {
window.open(ui.item.url);
}
}
}).each(function() {
$(this).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
return $("<li></li>")
.data("item.autocomplete", item)
.append($("<a'></a>").html(item.label))
.appendTo(ul);
};
});
function __highlight(s, t) {
var matcher = new RegExp("(" + $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(t) + ")", "ig");
return s.replace(matcher, "<span style='color:#144D94;font-weight: bold;'>$1</span>");
}
});
});
               </script>
              </div>
             </div>

_wr_re = function(k) {
var c = 0;
if (k.nodeType == 3) {
var n = k.data.indexOf("");
if (n >= 0) {
var m = document.createElement("span");
m.className = "WebRupee";
var e = k.splitText(n);
var o = e.splitText(1);
var p = e.cloneNode(true);
m.appendChild(p);
e.parentNode.replaceChild(m, e);
c = 1
}
} else {
if (k.nodeType == 1 && k.childNodes && !/(script|style)/i.test(k.tagName)) {
for (var l = 0; l < k.childNodes.length; ++l) {
l += _wr_re(k.childNodes[l])
}
}
}
return c
}

       $(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).on("makeSocialShareReady", function(event, data) {
var selector = $(data).find(".secArtShare ul li");
//selector.add($(data).find(".hover-social-media-bottom ul li"));
$(selector).on('click', function (e) {
e.preventDefault();
var shareUrl = $(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('share-url');
var shareText = $(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('share-text');
logEAE($(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('id'),"like");
if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-facebook')) {
openShareLink('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
} else if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-twitter')) {
openShareLink('https://twitter.com/share?text=' + shareText + '&url=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
} else if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-google-plus')) {
openShareLink('https://plus.google.com/share?url=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
} else if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-linkedin')) {
openShareLink('https://www.linkedin.com/cws/share?url=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
}
});
});
$(document).on('pageContentReady', function (event, content) {
$(document).trigger( "makeSocialShareReady", content );
});
});
$(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).trigger( "makeSocialShareReady", $('body') );
});
function openShareLink(pLink) {
var popUp = window.open(pLink, 'popupwindow', 'scrollbars=yes,width=740,height=400');
popUp.focus();
return false;
}
